new entry "Target_MindLeech_Modifiers"
type "SpellData"
data "SpellType" "Target"
using "Target_MindLeech"
data "ContainerSpells" ""
data "SpellFlags" "HasSomaticComponent;IsHarmful;IsSpell;IsLinkedSpellContainer;Temporary"
data "UseCosts" "ActionPoint:1;PsiPoint:1"
data "PowerLevel" "1"

new entry "Target_MindLeech_Rending"
type "SpellData"
data "SpellType" "Target"
using "Target_MindLeech_Modifiers"
